Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 210 (Apollo 15-17 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Jim Lawton, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP: ASSEMBLE REVISION 210 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY 
	BY NASA 2021112-161 17:11 MAR. 19,1971
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

022323,000028:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
022324,000029:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022325,000030:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022326,000031:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022327,000032:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022328,000033: 
022329,000034:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
022330,000035:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
022331,000036:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
022332,000037:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
022333,000038:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022334,000039: 
022335,000040:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
022336,000041:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022337,000042:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
022338,000043:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
022339,000044:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
022340,000045:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
022341,000046:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
022342,000047:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
022343,000048:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
022344,000049:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
022345,000050:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)    
022346,000051:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
022347,000052:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022348,000053:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022349,000054:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022350,000055:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022351,000056:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
022352,000057:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022353,000058:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
022354,000059:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022355,000060:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022356,000061:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
022357,000062:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022358,000063:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS -- A,Q,L
022359,000064: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
022360,000065: 
022361,000066: 33,2113                                           BANK     33                                    
022362,000067: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
022363,000068: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
022364,000069: 
022365,000070: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022366,000071: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
022367,000072: 24,2000  24,2000               PROG22             =        PROG20                                
022368,000073: 24,2000           05331        PROG20             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022369,000074: 24,2001           00004                           OCT      4                                     
022370,000075: 24,2002           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022371,000076: 24,2003           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022372,000077: 24,2004           02751                           TC       LUNSFCHK                              #  CHECK IF ON LUNAR SURFACE

022847,000552:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022848,000553:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
022849,000554:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
022850,000555:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022851,000556:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022852,000557: 
022853,000558:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
022854,000559:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
022855,000560:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
022856,000561:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
022857,000562:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022858,000563:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
022859,000564:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
022860,000565:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
022861,000566:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
022862,000567:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
022863,000568:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
022864,000569:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
022865,000570:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
022866,000571:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
022867,000572:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
022868,000573:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022869,000574:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022870,000575:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022871,000576:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022872,000577:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
022873,000578:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022874,000579:                                                                                                  #    NONE
022875,000580: 24,2462  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022876,000581: 24,2462                                           COUNT*   $$/P25                                
022877,000582: 24,2462           05331        PROG25             TC       2PHSCHNG                              
022878,000583: 24,2463           00004                           OCT      4                                     #  MAKE GROUP 4 INACTIVE (VERB 37)
022879,000584: 24,2464           05022                           OCT      05022                                 
022880,000585: 24,2465           26000                           OCT      26000                                 #  PRIORITY 26
022881,000586: 
022882,000587: 24,2466           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022883,000588: 24,2467           33757                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
022884,000589: 24,2470           05506                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022885,000590: 24,2471           00031                           ADRES    TRACKFLG                              #  SET TRACK FLAG
022886,000591: 24,2472           05506                           TC       UPFLAG                                
022887,000592: 24,2473           00006                           ADRES    P25FLAG                               #  SET P25FLAG
022888,000593: 24,2474           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              
022889,000594: 24,2475           00010                           ADRES    RNDVZFLG                              
022890,000595: 24,2476           05355        P25LEM1            TC       PHASCHNG                              
022891,000596: 24,2477           04022                           OCT      04022                                 
022892,000597: 24,2500           34734                           CAF      P25FLBIT                              
022893,000598: 24,2501           70074                           MASK     STATE                                 #  IS P25FLAG SET
022894,000599: 24,2502           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022895,000600: 24,2503           15146                           BZF      ENDOFJOB                              
022896,000601: 24,2504           34740                           CAF      TRACKBIT                              #  IS TRACKFLAG SET?

Page 519 

022898,000603: 24,2505           70075                           MASK     STATE      +1                         
022899,000604: 24,2506           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022900,000605: 24,2507           12515                           BZF      P25LMWT1                              #  NO-SKIP PHASE CHANGE AND WAIT 1 MINUTE
022901,000606: 24,2510           34750                           CAF      SEVEN                                 #  CALL R65 - FINE PREFERRED
022902,000607: 24,2511           55745                           TS       R65CNTR                               
022903,000608: 24,2512           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              #  TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE
022904,000609: 24,2513           46123                           CADR     R65LEM                                
022905,000610: 24,2514           02476                           TC       P25LEM1                               #  THEN GO CHECK FLAGS
022906,000611: 24,2515           32526        P25LMWT1           CAF      60SCNDS                               
022907,000612: 24,2516           05175                           TC       TWIDDLE                               #  WAIT ONE MINUTE THEN CHECK AGAIN

022921,000626:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022922,000627:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
022923,000628:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022924,000629: 
022925,000630:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
022926,000631:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
022927,000632:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
022928,000633:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022929,000634:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
022930,000635:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -

022934,000639:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022935,000640:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
022936,000641:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
022937,000642:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.

023122,000827:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
023123,000828:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023124,000829:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023125,000830:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023126,000831:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023127,000832: 
023128,000833:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
023129,000834:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
023130,000835:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023131,000836:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
023132,000837:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
023133,000838:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
023134,000839:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
023135,000840:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
023136,000841:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
023137,000842:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
023138,000843:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
023139,000844:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
023140,000845:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
023141,000846:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023142,000847:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
023143,000848:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
023144,000849:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
023145,000850:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023146,000851:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
023147,000852:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023148,000853:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
023149,000854:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023150,000855:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
023151,000856:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

023327,001032:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
023328,001033:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023329,001034:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023330,001035:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
023331,001036:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023332,001037: 
023333,001038:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023334,001039:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
023335,001040:                                                                                                  #           TC     R23LEM
023336,001041:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023337,001042:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL        R61LEM
023338,001043:                                                                                                  #    SETMINDB        GOPERF1
023339,001044:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
023340,001045:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
023341,001046:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF PROC  WILL CONTINUE R23
023342,001047:                                                                                                  #                               ,SELECTION OF TERM  WILL TERMINATE R23 +P20
023343,001048:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
023344,001049:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023345,001050:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023346,001051:                                                                                                  #    N.A.
023347,001052:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED-
023348,001053:                                                                                                  #    ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
023349,001054: 24,3220     1142                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
023350,001055: 24,3220                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
023351,001056: 24,3220           05506        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
023352,001057: 24,3221           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
023353,001058: 24,3222           00004                           INHINT                                         
023354,001059: 24,3223           04665                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
023355,001060: 24,3224           40141                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
023356,001061: 24,3225           00003                           RELINT                                         
023357,001062: 24,3226           34727        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
023358,001063: 24,3227           00006                           EXTEND

023360,001065: 24,3231           33270                           CAF      OCT205                                
023361,001066: 24,3232           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
023362,001067: 24,3233           20635                           CADR     GOPERF1

023364,001069: 24,3235           03237                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE

023366,001071: 24,3237           00004        R23LEM11           INHINT

023371,001076: 24,3244           40115                           CADR     RESTORDB                              #  ASTRONAUT SELECTED VALUE

023397,001102:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
023398,001103:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
023399,001104:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
023400,001105:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
023401,001106:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023402,001107: 
023403,001108:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
023404,001109:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
023405,001110:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
023406,001111:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
023407,001112:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
023408,001113:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
023409,001114:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
023410,001115:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
023411,001116:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023412,001117:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
023413,001118:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
023414,001119:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
023415,001120:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
023416,001121:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
023417,001122:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
023418,001123:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
023419,001124:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
023420,001125:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
023421,001126:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
023422,001127:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
023423,001128:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023424,001129:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
023425,001130:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
023426,001131:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
023427,001132: 24,3271  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
023428,001133: 24,3271                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
023429,001134: 24,3271           05506        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
023430,001135: 24,3272           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
023431,001136: 24,3273           05520                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
023432,001137: 24,3274           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
023433,001138: 24,3275           34746        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
023434,001139: 24,3276           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
023435,001140: 24,3277           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023436,001141: 24,3300           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
023437,001142: 24,3301           05355        R24LEM2            TC       PHASCHNG                              
023438,001143: 24,3302           04022                           OCT      04022

023440,001145: 24,3304           04607                           TC       BANKCALL                              
023441,001146: 24,3305           20477                           CADR     PRIODSPR                              
023442,001147: 24,3306           06043                           TC       GOTOV56                               
023443,001148: 24,3307           03313                           TC       R24END                                #  PROCEED EXIT R24 TO P20LEM1
023444,001149: 
023445,001150: 24,3310           03317                           TC       R24LEM3                               #  RECYCLE - CALL R61 TO MANEUVER S/C

023712,001417:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
023713,001418: 
023714,001419:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023715,001420:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
023716,001421:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
023717,001422:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
023718,001423:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
023719,001424:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
023720,001425:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023721,001426:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
023722,001427:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
023723,001428:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
023724,001429:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
023725,001430:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
023726,001431:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
023727,001432:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
023728,001433:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
023729,001434: 
023730,001435:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023731,001436:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
023732,001437:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
023733,001438: 
023734,001439:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023735,001440:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
023736,001441:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
023737,001442:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
023738,001443: 
023739,001444:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
023740,001445: 
023741,001446:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
023742,001447: 
023743,001448:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023744,001449: 
023745,001450:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
023746,001451:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)

023791,001496:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
023792,001497: 
023793,001498:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023794,001499:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
023795,001500:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
023796,001501:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
023797,001502:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
023798,001503:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
023799,001504:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
023800,001505:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
023801,001506:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
023802,001507:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
023803,001508:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
023804,001509:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
023805,001510:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
023806,001511:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
023807,001512:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
023808,001513:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
023809,001514:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
023810,001515:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
023811,001516:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
023812,001517:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
023813,001518: 
023814,001519:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023815,001520:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF
023816,001521: 
023817,001522:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D

023861,001566:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON

A vertical line is drawn next to the log section name and program name. 

023863,001568: 
023864,001569:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023865,001570: 
023866,001571:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WTIH
023867,001572:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
023868,001573:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
023869,001574:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
023870,001575:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
023871,001576:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
023872,001577:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
023873,001578:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
023874,001579:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
023875,001580:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
023876,001581:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
023877,001582:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
023878,001583: 
023879,001584:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER-ON AUTO
023880,001585:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
023881,001586:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
023882,001587: 
023883,001588:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023884,001589:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
023885,001590: 
023886,001591:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
023887,001592: 
023888,001593:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023889,001594:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023890,001595: 
023891,001596:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
023892,001597: 
023893,001598:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
023894,001599: 
023895,001600: 24,3337                                           BANK     24                                    
023896,001601: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
023897,001602: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
023898,001603: 
023899,001604: 25,2053  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023900,001605: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
023901,001606: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB

023903,001608: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.

023910,001615:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
023911,001616: 
023912,001617:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023913,001618:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
023914,001619:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
023915,001620:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
023916,001621:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
023917,001622:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
023918,001623:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
023919,001624:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
023920,001625:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
023921,001626:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
023922,001627:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
023923,001628:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
023924,001629:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
023925,001630:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
023926,001631:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
023927,001632:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
023928,001633: 
023929,001634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
023930,001635:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023931,001636:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
023932,001637: 
023933,001638:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
023934,001639: 
023935,001640:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023936,001641:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023937,001642: 
023938,001643:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRAKCER FAIL
023939,001644: 
023940,001645:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
023941,001646: 
023942,001647: 25,2062           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND

023944,001649: 25,2064           34744                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
023945,001650: 25,2065           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
023946,001651: 25,2066           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
023947,001652: 25,2067           05223                           TC       FIXDELAY

023983,001688:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
023984,001689:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023985,001690:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023986,001691:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
023987,001692:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
023988,001693:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
023989,001694:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
023990,001695:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
023991,001696:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
023992,001697:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
023993,001698:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
023994,001699:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
023995,001700:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
023996,001701:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
023997,001702:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
023998,001703:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
023999,001704:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
024000,001705:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
024001,001706:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
024002,001707:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024003,001708:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
024004,001709:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
024005,001710:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
024006,001711:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
024007,001712: 
024008,001713:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024009,001714:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
024010,001715:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
024011,001716: 
024012,001717:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024013,001718:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024014,001719: 
024015,001720:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024016,001721:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
024017,001722: 
024018,001723:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024019,001724:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024020,001725: 
024021,001726:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
024022,001727: 
024023,001728:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES

024070,001775:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
024071,001776: 
024072,001777:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
024073,001778:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
024074,001779:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
024075,001780:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
024076,001781:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
024077,001782:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
024078,001783:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
024079,001784:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024080,001785:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
024081,001786:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
024082,001787:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
024083,001788:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
024084,001789:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
024085,001790:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
024086,001791:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
024087,001792:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
024088,001793:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
024089,001794:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
024090,001795:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
024091,001796:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
024092,001797: 
024093,001798:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024094,001799:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
024095,001800:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
024096,001801:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
024097,001802:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
024098,001803: 
024099,001804:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INIITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024100,001805:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
024101,001806: 
024102,001807:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024103,001808:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
024104,001809: 
024105,001810:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024106,001811:                                                                                                  #  NONE

024160,001865:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
024161,001866: 
024162,001867:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024163,001868:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
024164,001869:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
024165,001870:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
024166,001871:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
024167,001872:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
024168,001873:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
024169,001874:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
024170,001875:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
024171,001876:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
024172,001877:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
024173,001878:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
024174,001879:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
024175,001880:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
024176,001881:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
024177,001882: 
024178,001883:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
024179,001884:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
024180,001885:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
024181,001886:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
024182,001887:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
024183,001888: 
024184,001889:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024185,001890:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
024186,001891: 
024187,001892:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_

024192,001897:

024196,001901:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)

024248,001953:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
024249,001954: 
024250,001955:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024251,001956:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
024252,001957:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
024253,001958:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
024254,001959:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
024255,001960:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
024256,001961:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
024257,001962:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
024258,001963:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
024259,001964:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
024260,001965:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
024261,001966:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
024262,001967:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
024263,001968:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024264,001969: 
024265,001970:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024266,001971:                                                                                                  #  L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
024267,001972:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
024268,001973: 
024269,001974:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024270,001975:                                                                                                  #  TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
024271,001976:                                                                                                  #  (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).

024354,002059:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
024355,002060: 
024356,002061:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024357,002062:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
024358,002063:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF-SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
024359,002064:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
024360,002065:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
024361,002066:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
024362,002067:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE CORRDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
024363,002068:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
024364,002069:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
024365,002070:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
024366,002071:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
024367,002072:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
024368,002073:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
024369,002074:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
024370,002075:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
024371,002076:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
024372,002077:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
024373,002078:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
024374,002079:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
024375,002080:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
024376,002081:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
024377,002082:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
024378,002083:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
024379,002084: 
024380,002085:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024381,002086:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
024382,002087:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
024383,002088:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024384,002089:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
024385,002090: 
024386,002091:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024387,002092:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
024388,002093: 
024389,002094:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024390,002095:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
024391,002096:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
024392,002097: 
024393,002098:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024394,002099:                                                                                                  #     NONE
024395,002100: 
024396,002101:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
024397,002102: 
024398,002103:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
024399,002104:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
024400,002105:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
