024440,002145:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
024441,002146: 
024442,002147:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
024443,002148:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
024444,002149:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024445,002150:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
024446,002151:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
024447,002152:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
024448,002153:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
024449,002154:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
024450,002155:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
024451,002156:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
024452,002157:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
024453,002158:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
024454,002159:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
024455,002160:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
024456,002161:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
024457,002162:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
024458,002163:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
024459,002164:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
024460,002165:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
024461,002166:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
024462,002167:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
024463,002168: 
024464,002169:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024465,002170:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
024466,002171: 
024467,002172:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024468,002173:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)

024612,002317:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
024613,002318: 
024614,002319:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024615,002320:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
024616,002321:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
024617,002322:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
024618,002323:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
024619,002324:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
024620,002325:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
024621,002326:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
024622,002327:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
024623,002328:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024624,002329:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, AN EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
024625,002330:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
024626,002331:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
024627,002332:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
024628,002333:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
024629,002334:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
024630,002335:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
024631,002336:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
024632,002337:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
024633,002338:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
024634,002339:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
024635,002340:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
024636,002341:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
024637,002342:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
024638,002343:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
024639,002344:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
024640,002345: 
024641,002346:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024642,002347:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
024643,002348:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
024644,002349:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
024645,002350: 
024646,002351:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024647,002352:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
024648,002353: 
024649,002354:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024650,002355:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
024651,002356: 
024652,002357:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
024653,002358: 
024654,002359:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
024655,002360:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
024656,002361: 
024657,002362:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
024658,002363:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
024659,002364:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
024660,002365: 
024661,002366: 25,2564           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

Page 563 

024707,002412:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
024708,002413: 
024709,002414:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024710,002415:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
024711,002416:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
024712,002417:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
024713,002418:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
024714,002419:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
024715,002420:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
024716,002421:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
024717,002422:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
024718,002423:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
024719,002424:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
024720,002425:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
024721,002426:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
024722,002427:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
024723,002428:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
024724,002429:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
024725,002430:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
024726,002431:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
024727,002432:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
024728,002433:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
024729,002434:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024730,002435:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
024731,002436:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
024732,002437:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
024733,002438:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
024734,002439:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
024735,002440:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
024736,002441:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
024737,002442:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
024738,002443:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, TEH RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
024739,002444:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
024740,002445:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
024741,002446:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
024742,002447:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
024743,002448:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
024744,002449:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
024745,002450:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
024746,002451:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
024747,002452: 
024748,002453:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024749,002454:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
024750,002455: 
024751,002456:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024752,002457:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
024753,002458:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
024754,002459: 
024755,002460:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024756,002461:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
024757,002462:

Page 564 

024759,002464:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
024760,002465:                                                                                                  #  NONE
024761,002466:

024828,002533: 25,2712           74731                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
024829,002534: 25,2713           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT

025041,002746:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE, WHICH IS INITIATED BY A RADAR RUPT, PROCESSES THE RADAR DATA AND UPDATES THE APPROPRIATE

025684,003389:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
025685,003390:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
025686,003391: 
025687,003392: 
025688,003393:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025689,003394: 
025690,003395:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
025691,003396:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
025692,003397:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
025693,003398: 
025694,003399:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
025695,003400: 
025696,003401: 
025697,003402:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
025698,003403: 
025699,003404: 
025700,003405:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025701,003406: 
025702,003407:                                                                                                  #         RRDOT    LPS20.1
025703,003408:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
025704,003409:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
025705,003410:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
025706,003411:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
025707,003412: 
025708,003413: 
025709,003414:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
025710,003415: 
025711,003416:                                                                                                  #               00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
025712,003417:                                                                                                  #               00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
025713,003418: 
025714,003419: 
025715,003420:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
025716,003421:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
025717,003422: 
025718,003423: 
025719,003424:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR(USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
025720,003425:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING(TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29(USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
025721,003426: 
025722,003427:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
025723,003428: 
025724,003429:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
025725,003430:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025726,003431:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
025727,003432:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
025728,003433:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
025729,003434: 
025730,003435: 
025731,003436:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025732,003437: 
025733,003438:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 588 

025735,003440:                                                                                                  #      1)RR RANGE SCALED 9.38 FT. PER BIT ON THE LOW SCALE AND 75.04 FT. PER BIT ON THE HIGH SCALE
025736,003441:                                                                                                  #      2)RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
025737,003442: 
025738,003443:                                                                                                  #     THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX,CDUY,CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
025739,003444: 
025740,003445:

025952,003657:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
025953,003658:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
025954,003659:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
025955,003660: 
025956,003661:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025957,003662: 
025958,003663:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
025959,003664:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
025960,003665:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
025961,003666: 
025962,003667:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025963,003668:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
025964,003669:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
025965,003670:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
025966,003671:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
025967,003672:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
025968,003673:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
025969,003674: 
025970,003675: 
025971,003676:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025972,003677:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
025973,003678:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RADARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
025974,003679: 
025975,003680:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025976,003681:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025977,003682:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025978,003683:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
025979,003684:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025980,003685:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025981,003686: 
025982,003687: 
025983,003688:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025984,003689:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
025985,003690:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
025986,003691:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025987,003692:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025988,003693:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
025989,003694:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
025990,003695:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
025991,003696:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
025992,003697:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
025993,003698:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
025994,003699:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
025995,003700:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
025996,003701:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
025997,003702:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
025998,003703: 
025999,003704:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026000,003705:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
026001,003706:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)

026392,004097: 26,3205           50644                                    R22LEM93                              
026393,004098:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026394,004099: 
026395,004100:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
026396,004101:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
026397,004102:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
026398,004103: 
026399,004104:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026400,004105:                                                                                                  #   INTSTALL  LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
026401,004106:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
026402,004107: 
026403,004108:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026404,004109:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
026405,004110:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
026406,004111:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
026407,004112:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
026408,004113:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
026409,004114:

Page 594 

026411,004116:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026412,004117:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
026413,004118:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
026414,004119:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
026415,004120:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
026416,004121:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
026417,004122:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
026418,004123: 
026419,004124: 
026420,004125: 26,3206           77624        LSR22.4            CALL                                           
026421,004126: 26,3207           27447                                    INTSTALL

026624,004329:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
026625,004330:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
026626,004331: 
026627,004332: 
026628,004333:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026629,004334: 
026630,004335:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
026631,004336:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
026632,004337:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
026633,004338:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
026634,004339: 
026635,004340: 
026636,004341:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
026637,004342: 
026638,004343: 
026639,004344:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026640,004345: 
026641,004346:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
026642,004347:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
026643,004348:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
026644,004349:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
026645,004350:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
026646,004351: 
026647,004352: 
026648,004353:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
026649,004354: 
026650,004355: 
026651,004356:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026652,004357: 
026653,004358:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
026654,004359:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
026655,004360:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGNT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
026656,004361: 
026657,004362:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
026658,004363:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
026659,004364:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
026660,004365:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026661,004366: 
026662,004367:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
026663,004368:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
026664,004369:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
026665,004370:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
026666,004371:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
026667,004372: 
026668,004373: 
026669,004374: 26,3441                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24
